] ),

comp( 
[ 
subComp(ttrig, Nil, when, the LSC, is greater than, [the NoSailing requests, ], when the LSC is greater than the NoSailing requests ),
subComp(in-time, every, , 18, seconds, [], every 18 seconds),
subComp(v-time, for, at least, 17, seconds, [], for at least 17 seconds)
] ),

[

subComp(in-time, every, , 23, seconds, [], every 23 seconds)
] )

]

Req-497:  the standstill request flag shall be sent to the NoSailing requests  within at most 10 seconds every at least 28 seconds , if the quality signal whose index exceeds 7 exceeds the defined position for at most 25 seconds , before the vehicle speed setpoint is greater than the brake fault state for at most 15 seconds  .
[
comp( 
[ 
subComp(act, Nil, Nil, the standstill request flag, shall be sent, [the NoSailing requests, ], the standstill request flag shall be sent to the NoSailing requests),
subComp(pre-time, within, at most, 10, seconds, [], within at most 10 seconds),
subComp(in-time, every, at least, 28, seconds, [], every at least 28 seconds)
] ),

comp( 
[ 
subComp(cond, Nil, if, the quality signal, exceeds, [the defined position, ], if the quality signal exceeds the defined position ),
subComp(hidden, the quality signal, whose, index, exceeds, [7, ], the quality signal whose index exceeds 7 ),
subComp(v-time, for, at most, 25, seconds, [], for at most 25 seconds)
] ),

comp( 
[ 
subComp(condScope, Nil, before, the vehicle speed setpoint, is greater than, [the brake fault state, ], before the vehicle speed setpoint is greater than the brake fault state ),
subComp(v-time, for, at most, 15, seconds, [], for at most 15 seconds)
] )

]
===========================================

%%%
Req-498: if the quality signal whose index exceeds 6 is [True] ,  the transmission error shall be received from the engine error  within at least 23 seconds , before the vehicle speed setpoint is greater than the engine error for 20 seconds , before the vehicle speed setpoint whose index is above 6 is less than the defined position  .
[
comp( 
[ 
subComp(cond, Nil, if, the quality signal, is, [[True], ], if the quality signal is [True] ),
subComp(hidden, the quality signal, whose, index, exceeds, [6, ], the quality signal whose index exceeds 6 )
] ),

comp( 
[ 
subComp(act, Nil, Nil, the transmission error, shall be received, [the engine error, ], the transmission error shall be received from the engine error),
subComp(pre-time, within, at least, 23, seconds, [], within at least 23 seconds)
] ),

comp( 
[ 
subComp(condScope, Nil, before, the vehicle speed setpoint, is greater than, [the engine error, ], before the vehicle speed setpoint is greater than the engine error ),
subComp(v-time, for, , 20, seconds, [], for 20 seconds)
] ),

comp( 
[ 
subComp(condScope, Nil, before, the vehicle speed setpoint, is less than, [the defined position, ], before the vehicle speed setpoint is less than the defined position ),
subComp(hidden, the vehicle speed setpoint, whose, index, is above, [6, ], the vehicle speed setpoint whose index is above 6 )
] )

]

%%%
Req-499:  the sailing request shall be received from the transmission error  for 13 seconds , if the sailing request whose index is 7 is less than the LSC within at most 4 seconds  .
[
comp( 
[ 
subComp(act, Nil, Nil, the sailing request, shall be received, [the transmission error, ], the sailing request shall be received from the transmission error),
subComp(v-time, for, , 13, seconds, [], for 13 seconds)
] ),

comp( 
[ 
subComp(cond, Nil, if, the sailing request, is less than, [the LSC, ], if the sailing request is less than the LSC ),
subComp(hidden, the sailing request, whose, index, is, [7, ], the sailing request whose index is 7 ),
subComp(pre-time, within, at most, 4, seconds, [], within at most 4 seconds)
] )

]
===========================================

%%%
Req-500: if the IDC inhibitor that is greater than 3 is above the steering wheel angle for at least 5 seconds within at least 29 seconds , after the vehicle speed quality factor that exceeds 5 exceeds the engine error , when the vehicle speed quality factor that equals 6 is less than the IDC inhibitor every at least 26 seconds ,  the sailing termination shall be turned to the vehicle speed quality factor  within 16 seconds  .
[
comp( 
[ 
subComp(cond, Nil, if, the IDC inhibitor, is above, [the steering wheel angle, ], if the IDC inhibitor is above the steering wheel angle ),
subComp(hidden, the IDC inhibitor, that, Nil, is greater than, [3, ], the IDC inhibitor that is greater than 3 ),
subComp(v-time, for, at least, 5, seconds, [], for at least 5 seconds),
subComp(pre-time, within, at least, 29, seconds, [], within at least 29 seconds)
] ),

comp( 
[ 
subComp(condScope, Nil, after, the vehicle speed quality factor, exceeds, [the engine error, ], after the vehicle speed quality factor exceeds the engine error ),
subComp(hidden, the vehicle speed quality factor, that, Nil, exceeds, [5, ], the vehicle speed quality factor that exceeds 5 )
] ),

comp( 
[ 
subComp(ttrig, Nil, when, the vehicle speed quality factor, is less than, [the IDC inhibitor, ], when the vehicle speed quality factor is less than the IDC inhibitor ),
subComp(hidden, the vehicle speed quality factor, that, Nil, equals, [6, ], the vehicle speed quality factor that equals 6 ),
subComp(in-time, every, at least, 26, seconds, [], every at least 26 seconds)
] ),

comp( 
[ 
subComp(act, Nil, Nil, the sailing termination, shall be turned, [the vehicle speed quality factor, ], the sailing termination shall be turned to the vehicle speed quality factor),
subComp(pre-time, within, , 16, seconds, [], within 16 seconds)
] )

]
